posted:Posted May 29, 2024
msg:Pros:
- Very convenient location, a couple of minutes walk to the West Lake.
- The lobby is spotless, check in/out is smooth.
- We went with a driver/tour guide (Zhu Feng) associated with the hotel who was very helpful, drove us around the lake for most of a day in pouring rain.
- Bellman is very helpful with loading luggage (he needs to work out more though :).
- Breakfast is good, but not great.

Cons
- The room is a little outdated, needs some maintenance work.
- The AC is the worst. The one in our room was blasting air all day long, but can barely keep the temperate at 25 C (77 F).
- The gym is pretty crappy. Looks like it's been rented out for external use, and it's not very clean or well maintained.

Overall got a good bone but needs some management shakeup and remodeling.

msg:It‚Äôs hard to describe this hotel, so everyone must be careful when booking!

Before check-in, hotel staff will inexplicably call you and send you a WeChat message to tell you that the room has been upgraded and that the guest service will be provided.
But the reality was much worse. We were given a very poor room, and we couldn't solve the problems we encountered. On the last day, we came to ask for positive reviews, saying, "The leader insists on positive reviews, and we won't be allowed to leave work if we don't give positive reviews."

1. About the room:
We arrived at night that day, and we felt bad the moment we opened the room. The room was filled with mirrors, almost the entire room was filled with mirrors. There is a row of mirrors in the corridor, the wardrobe in the bathroom, and the doors of the wardrobe are all covered with mirrors. The mirror in the corridor corresponds to the mirror in the closet in the bathroom. The pattern is very strange, you can experience it yourself.
There are no illustrations or descriptions of these things in the hotel room introduction. When I asked the front desk, the front desk was very vague. It just feels like I am deliberately avoiding it.
In the toilet room, the toilet seat is broken and covered with dust. At a glance, it looks dirty. There is a box of toilet paper next to the toilet. There is only one piece of paper in it, and there is also a layer of dust on the toilet paper box. If someone checked out this room before and the guest room came in for cleaning, would these hygiene issues go unnoticed? Why were the consumables not added in time? So obviously this room must have been unoccupied for a long, long time.
So we immediately communicated with the previous concierge and guest service, and the reply he gave was that all rooms were of this type.

After we returned to the hotel after dinner, the front desk said they would change a room for us. Unexpectedly, it was the same room as before. Before we went out, we made a clear request for a clean room with so many mirrors, but the front desk changed us to a room that was exactly the same as the original one. So what does this mean?

Later, after a long period of communication, we moved to a similar room next door. Since it was already past 11 o'clock in the middle of the night, we only stayed for two nights, so we did not communicate with them again.
There was a problem with the room. We spent a lot of time looking up and down the room at the front desk. In fact, the room we changed to in the end also had problems. I felt a little uncomfortable. It was already almost 12 o'clock after the room change that day. It was very terrible. Tired. So I don‚Äôt want to communicate with them anymore in the future.

2. About room hygiene
The new room we moved to was also very unsanitary. The exhaust system was very weak and the bathroom was always filled with a faint smell of cigarette smoke.
I don't know if it was alcohol or something, but there was a big stain on the bedside.
There was visible hair on the sheets.
The toiletries in the bathroom were placed in a wooden box, but the wooden box had become moldy and water-infested. A very dirty feeling.
There was probably a clothes-drying rope in the bathroom, but it was modified.
The door's safety lock has been modified and has obvious traces.
The whole room feels very dark even if all the lights are turned on.
Maybe it‚Äôs just that it‚Äôs been open for a long time, and many things have been patched, making the experience of staying here really bad.

When we went out the next day, there was no need for housekeeping, and there was no sign saying it would be cleaned immediately. However, it was still cleaned when we came back in the evening.

3. Breakfast
There are very few types of breakfast, and some porridge and the like are cold. Although it is a buffet breakfast, after walking around, I have no appetite at all.
For Intercontinental hotels with similar prices, Wyndham is really far behind. Therefore, it is recommended that if you are booking a hotel, there is no need to book a double breakfast.
There are only a few people eating breakfast, which shows how high the occupancy rate is.

In general, it is called an old hotel, and it is indeed an old hotel! The main theme is "old", and the soft furnishings in the room can really be replaced.
In terms of price, it‚Äôs about the same price. I still recommend you to choose Intercontinental or West Lake Shangri-La, or the slightly more expensive Grand Hyatt and Shangri-La in the city.
The only advantage of this hotel is that it is close to the West Lake, making it easier to walk to the West Lake. But in other terms, whether it is facilities, rooms or hotel services, they are far from their pricing.

Another note: On the last day we checked out and went to pick up the luggage stored at the front desk, we were dragged back to ask for a good review. They also forcibly took our luggage and said they would send us out. This really made the guests who checked in feel very uncomfortable.
